SET_PREDICTIONS 5728848cff5b5019007da29a = ['s', 'system', 'since', 'frederick', 'this', 'actual', 'guarantee', 'position', 'well', 'their', 'rich', 'misleading', 'term', 'semu', 'than', 'people', 'usage', 'of', 'so', 'were', 'standing', 'less', 'classes', 'w', 'and', 'for', 'fourclass', 'entitled', 'in', 'indication', 'within', 'mongol', 'historian', 'power', 'chinese', 'person', 'who', 'just', 'privilege', 'institutionally', 'wrote', 'but', 'poverty', 'not', 'that', 'mote', 'there', 'entailed', 'legally', 'socially', 'social', 'to', 'they', 'was', 'lived', 'degrees', 'treated', 'ill', 'while', 'wealth', 'which']
